Rust Compiler's Relationship with Servo's Selectors\\n\\n**No Direct Dependency**: The Rust compiler's `compiler/` and `library/` crates do NOT depend on or import Servo's `selectors` crate.\\n\\n**Testing Integration**: \\n- `src/tools/cargotest/main.rs` (lines 72-83) includes Servo as a test case\\n- Line 79: `packages: &[\\\"selectors\\\"]` - Tests only the selectors crate from Servo\\n- This is for verification that Servo's selectors package compiles with the Rust compiler being tested\\n\\n### 3. Exports the `bridge` module as public API\\n\\n**Bridge Implementation Files**:\\n- `library/proc_macro/src/bridge/mod.rs` - Core bridge definition\\n  - Lines 18-104: Defines the `with_api!` macro that describes the server RPC API\\n  - Server-side implementation\\n  - Defines `HandleStore<S: Types>` for managing handles\\n  - Implements encoding/decoding traits for inter-process communication\\n  - Provides server-side traits for proc macro execution\\n\\n- `library/proc_macro/src/bridge/client.rs` - Client-side implementation\\n  - Implements bridge entry points for proc macro clients\\n  - Manages thread-local bridge state via `Bridge::with()`\\n  - Provides methods like `def_site()`, `call_site()`, etc.\\n\\n**Key Dependency**: The bridge uses a closed-channel design with handle-based serialization to safely interface between two copies of `proc_macro` built by different compilers (e.g., stage0/bin/rustc vs stage1/bin/rustc during bootstrap).\\n\\n### Architectural Summary\\n\\nThe shared code between Rust and Servo follows a clear separation:\\n1. **Servo** depends on external styling crates from `servo/stylo` repository\\n2. **Rust compiler** does not depend on these crates directly but can test compatibility via cargotest\\n3. **Proc_macro bridge** is a Rust standard library component that enables build scripts and proc macros to communicate with the compiler, which Servo uses for its build system\\n\\nThis architecture allows Rust and Servo to share styling infrastructure (through the separate stylo repository) while maintaining independence -
